i <= newPhone.length; i++) {\n        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 80));\n        setLocalPhone(newPhone.substring(0, i));\n        onChange(newPhone.substring(0, i));\n      }\n      \n      setFilling(false);\n      \n      if (newPhone.length === 10) {\n        speak(\"Phone number complete! Please say your phone number.\");\n    }\n  }, [localPhone, onChange, speak, onNext]);\n\n  const toggleListening = () => {\n    if (isListening) {\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n      setIsListening(false);\n    } else {\n      startListening();\n    }\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => {\n    if (p.length <= 3) return p;\n    if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`;\n    return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\n  };\n\n  const handleChange = (value: string) => {\n    const digits = value.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n    setLocalPhone(digits);\n    onChange(digits);\n  };\n\n  const isValid = localPhone.length === 10;\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\n      {/* Header */}\n      <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n        <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\ud83c\udfd7\ufe0f</span>\n        <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0 5px' }}>Builder Phone Number</h3>\n        <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Say your digits: \"seven zero three...\"</p>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Phone Input */}\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\n        <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>+1</span>\n        <input\n          ref={inputRef}\n          id=\"builder-phone-input\"\n          type=\"tel\"\n          value={formatPhone(localPhone)}\n          onChange={e => handleChange(e.target.value)}\n          placeholder=\"000-000-0000\"\n          className={filling ? recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n      setIsListening(false);\\n    } else {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.start();\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  if (!isOpen) return Click Send OTP to continue.\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Voice commands\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    if (lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('send') || lower.includes('continue')) {\\n      if (localPhone.length === 10) {\\n        onNext();\\n      }\\n    }\\n    if (lower.includes('clear') || lower.includes('reset')) {\\n      setLocalPhone('');\\n      onChange('');\\n      speak(\\\"Cleared. Say upload or next to continue.`);\\n    setTimeout(() => startListening(), 1500);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (SR) {\\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n        let text = '';\\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; };\\n    }\\n    return () => recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n  }, [isListening]);\\n\\n  const startListening = () => { try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); setIsListening(true); } catch (e) {} };\\n  const toggleListening = () => { if (isListening) { recognitionRef.current?.stop(); setIsListening(false); } else { startListening(); } };\\n\\n  const handleUpload = async (file: File) => {\\n    if (!file) return;\\n    setUploading(true); setStatus('uploading'); setProgress(10); setFileName(file.name);\\n    speak(`Uploading ${file.name}`);\\n    onFileSelect(file);\\n\\n    const formData = new FormData();\\n    formData.append('file', file);\\n\\n    try {\\n      setProgress(30);\\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/upload/pdf', { method: 'POST', body: formData });\\n      setProgress(70);\\n      const data = await response.json();\\n      setProgress(100);\\n      setStatus('success');\\n      onProductsExtracted(data.products || []);\\n      speak(\\\"Upload successful!\\\");\\n    } catch (err) {\\n      setStatus('error');\\n      speak(\\\"Upload failed. STEP 8: Create BuilderFlow.tsx (main flow using separate components)\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\ncat => void; onBack: () => void; }\\n\\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'profile' | 'dashboard' | 'upload' | 'complete';\\nconst STEPS: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'complete'];\\nconst LABELS = ['Phone', 'Verify', 'Profile', 'Dashboard', 'Upload', 'Done'];\\nconst THEME = { primary: '#1e3a5f', secondary: '#0f1c2e', accent: '#f59e0b' };\\n\\nconst BuilderFlow: React.FC<Props> = ({ onClose, onBack }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');\\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\\n  const [companyName, setCompanyName] = useState('');\\n  const [profile, setProfile] = useState('');\\n  const [products, setProducts] = useState<any[]>([]);\\n\\n  const synth = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\\n  const speak = useCallback((t: string) => { synth?.cancel(); const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(t); u.rate = 0.95; synth?.speak(u); }, [synth]);\\n\\n  const goNext = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i < STEPS.length - 1) setStep(STEPS[i + 1]); };\\n  const goBack = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i > 0) setStep(STEPS[i - 1]); else onBack(); };\\n\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n\\n  const renderStep = () => {\\n    switch (step) {\\n      case 'phone': return <BuilderPhone phone={phone} onChange={setPhone} onNext={goNext} speak={speak} />;\\n      case 'otp': return <BuilderOTP phone={phone} otp={otp} onChange={setOtp} onVerify={goNext} speak={speak} />;\\n      case 'profile': return <BuilderProfile profile={profile} companyName={companyName} onChange={setProfile} onCompanyChange={setCompanyName} onSave={goNext} speak={speak} />;\\n      case 'dashboard': return <BuilderDashboard companyName={companyName} onContinue={goNext} speak={speak} />;\\n      case 'upload': return <BuilderUpload onFileSelect={() => {}} onProductsExtracted={(p) => { setProducts(p); goNext(); }} speak={speak} />;\\n      case 'complete': return (\\n        <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 40 }}>\\n          <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83c\\udf89</span>\\n          <h2 style={{ color: THEME.accent }}>Setup Complete!</h2>\\n          <p style={{ color: '#888' }}>Your builder account is ready.</p>\\n          <button onClick={onClose} style={{ padding: '14px 40px', marginTop: 20, background: THEME.accent, border: 'none', borderRadius: 30, color: '#000', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer' }}>Go to Dashboard</button>\\n        </div>\\n      );\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ position: 'fixed', inset: 0, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', zIndex: 10000, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', padding: 20 }}>\\n      <div style={{ background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.primary}, ${THEME.secondary})`, borderRadius: 20, width: '100%', maxWidth: 600, maxHeight: '90vh', overflow: 'hidden', border: `2px solid ${THEME.accent}40` }}>\\n        {/* Header */}\\n        <div style={{ padding: '16px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}30`, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 14 }}>\\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\\ud83c\\udfd7\\ufe0f</span>\\n            <div>\\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Builder Setup</h2>\\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1}/{STEPS.length} \\u2022 {LABELS[stepIndex]}</span>\\n            </div>\\n          </div>\\n          <button onClick={onClose} style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: 'none', color: '#fff', width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: '50%', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>\\u2715</button>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Progress */}\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: 4, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\\n          {STEPS.map((_, i) => (<div key={i} style={{ flex: 1, height: 4, borderRadius:
